>26&nbsp;But&nbsp;when&nbsp;the&nbsp;blade&nbsp;was&nbsp;sprung&nbsp;up,&nbsp;and&nbsp;brought&nbsp;forth&nbsp;fruit,&nbsp;then&nbsp;appeared&nbsp;the&nbsp;tares&nbsp;also.</span><span >27&nbsp;So&nbsp;the&nbsp;servants&nbsp;of&nbsp;the&nbsp;householder&nbsp;came&nbsp;and&nbsp;said&nbsp;unto&nbsp;him,&nbsp;Sir,&nbsp;didst&nbsp;not&nbsp;thou&nbsp;sow&nbsp;good&nbsp;seed&nbsp;in&nbsp;thy&nbsp;field?&nbsp;from&nbsp;whence&nbsp;then&nbsp;hath&nbsp;it&nbsp;tares?</span><span >29&nbsp;But&nbsp;he&nbsp;said,&nbsp;Nay;&nbsp;lest&nbsp;while&nbsp;ye&nbsp;gather&nbsp;up&nbsp;the&nbsp;tares,&nbsp;ye&nbsp;root&nbsp;up&nbsp;also&nbsp;the&nbsp;wheat&nbsp;with&nbsp;them.</span><span >30&nbsp;Let&nbsp;both&nbsp;grow&nbsp;together&nbsp;until&nbsp;the&nbsp;harvest:&nbsp;and&nbsp;in&nbsp;the&nbsp;time&nbsp;of&nbsp;harvest&nbsp;I&nbsp;will&nbsp;say&nbsp;to&nbsp;the&nbsp;reapers,&nbsp;Gather&nbsp;ye&nbsp;together&nbsp;first&nbsp;the&nbsp;tares,&nbsp;and&nbsp;bind&nbsp;them&nbsp;in&nbsp;bundles&nbsp;to&nbsp;burn&nbsp;them:&nbsp;but&nbsp;gather&nbsp;the&nbsp;wheat&nbsp;into&nbsp;my&nbsp;barn.</span><span >40&nbsp;As&nbsp;therefore&nbsp;the&nbsp;tares&nbsp;are&nbsp;gathered&nbsp;and&nbsp;burned&nbsp;in&nbsp;the&nbsp;fire;&nbsp;so&nbsp;shall&nbsp;it&nbsp;be&nbsp;in&nbsp;the&nbsp;end&nbsp;of&nbsp;this&nbsp;world.</span><span >&nbsp;are&nbsp;the&nbsp;children&nbsp;of&nbsp;the&nbsp;devil&nbsp;or&nbsp;the&nbsp;wicked&nbsp;one&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p17 style="margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; " ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >4&#160;Seed&nbsp;is&nbsp;to&nbsp;bear&nbsp;fruit.&nbsp;If&nbsp;it&nbsp;does&nbsp;not,&nbsp;it&nbsp;is&nbsp;either&nbsp;</span><span class="15" style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-style:italic; >The&nbsp;devil&nbsp;operates&nbsp;under&nbsp;the&nbsp;cover&nbsp;of&nbsp;darkness&nbsp;and&nbsp;deception.</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p17 style="margin-left:36.0000pt; text-indent:-18.0000pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; mso-list:l17 level1 lfo32; " ><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><span style='mso-list:Ignore; ' >1.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >The&nbsp;devil&nbsp;does&nbsp;his&nbsp;work&nbsp;to&nbsp;sow&nbsp;wicked&nbsp;or&nbsp;lawless&nbsp;people&nbsp;in&nbsp;the&nbsp;world&nbsp;and&nbsp;to&nbsp;do&nbsp;it&nbsp;secretly&nbsp;so&nbsp;that&nbsp;they&nbsp;will&nbsp;not&nbsp;be&nbsp;noticed&nbsp;&#160;</span><span >2.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >The&nbsp;devil&nbsp;sows&nbsp;in&nbsp;the&nbsp;same&nbsp;field&nbsp;as&nbsp;the&nbsp;Lord.&nbsp;The&nbsp;bad&nbsp;are&nbsp;sown&nbsp;among&nbsp;the&nbsp;good.&nbsp;The&nbsp;devil's&nbsp;method&nbsp;is&nbsp;counterfeit&nbsp;and&nbsp;imitation.&nbsp;&nbsp;Some&nbsp;within&nbsp;the&nbsp;world&nbsp;and&nbsp;within&nbsp;the&nbsp;church&nbsp;have&nbsp;not&nbsp;been&nbsp;sown&nbsp;by&nbsp;the&nbsp;Lord.&nbsp;They&nbsp;may&nbsp;be&nbsp;in&nbsp;the&nbsp;world&nbsp;and&nbsp;in&nbsp;the&nbsp;(church);&nbsp;they&nbsp;may&nbsp;even&nbsp;look&nbsp;like&nbsp;they&nbsp;belong&nbsp;to&nbsp;Him,&nbsp;but&nbsp;they&nbsp;do&nbsp;not.</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p17 style="margin-left:36.0000pt; text-indent:-18.0000pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; mso-list:l17 level1 lfo32; " ><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><span style='mso-list:Ignore; ' >3.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >The&nbsp;devil&nbsp;is&nbsp;a&nbsp;sworn&nbsp;enemy&nbsp;to&nbsp;Christ,&nbsp;to&nbsp;the&nbsp;world,&nbsp;and&nbsp;to&nbsp;all&nbsp;good.&nbsp;He&nbsp;is&nbsp;the&nbsp;sworn&nbsp;enemy&nbsp;of&nbsp;man,&nbsp;to&nbsp;his&nbsp;peace,&nbsp;and&nbsp;to&nbsp;the&nbsp;fulfillment&nbsp;of&nbsp;his&nbsp;purpose&nbsp;and&nbsp;life&nbsp;on&nbsp;earth.&nbsp;Whatever&nbsp;power&nbsp;he&nbsp;uses&nbsp;on&nbsp;earth&nbsp;is&nbsp;the&nbsp;same&nbsp;as&nbsp;the&nbsp;power&nbsp;used&nbsp;by&nbsp;wicked&nbsp;men:&nbsp;it&nbsp;is&nbsp;usurped&nbsp;and&nbsp;unjust&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p17 style="margin-left:36.0000pt; text-indent:-18.0000pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; mso-list:l17 level1 lfo32; " ><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><span style='mso-list:Ignore; ' >4.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >One&nbsp;reason&nbsp;so&nbsp;many&nbsp;tares&nbsp;are&nbsp;sown&nbsp;is&nbsp;because&nbsp;so&nbsp;many&nbsp;righteous&nbsp;are&nbsp;sleeping&nbsp;when&nbsp;they&nbsp;should&nbsp;be&nbsp;watching&nbsp;over&nbsp;the&nbsp;field.&nbsp;Satan&nbsp;never&nbsp;sleeps;&nbsp;he&nbsp;is&nbsp;ever&nbsp;awake&nbsp;for&nbsp;every&nbsp;opportunity.</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p17 style="margin-left:36.0000pt; text-indent:-18.0000pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; mso-list:l17 level1 lfo32; " ><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><span style='mso-list:Ignore; ' >5.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >"He&nbsp;went&nbsp;his&nbsp;way."&nbsp;Satan&nbsp;does&nbsp;not&nbsp;want&nbsp;to&nbsp;be&nbsp;known&nbsp;as&nbsp;the&nbsp;sower&nbsp;of&nbsp;wicked&nbsp;men.&nbsp;In&nbsp;fact,&nbsp;he&nbsp;wants&nbsp;the&nbsp;wicked&nbsp;to&nbsp;disclaim&nbsp;him,&nbsp;never&nbsp;to&nbsp;confess&nbsp;that&nbsp;he&nbsp;is&nbsp;their&nbsp;"father"&nbsp;(John&nbsp;8:44).&nbsp;The&nbsp;tares&nbsp;are&nbsp;"in&nbsp;the&nbsp;Lord's&nbsp;field"&nbsp;professing&nbsp;that&nbsp;they&nbsp;belong&nbsp;to&nbsp;God,&nbsp;but&nbsp;they&nbsp;are&nbsp;deceived&nbsp;(2&nbsp;Cor.&nbsp;11:13-14).</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p17 style="margin-left:36.0000pt; text-indent:-18.0000pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; mso-list:l17 level1 lfo32; " ><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><span style='mso-list:Ignore; ' >6.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >The&nbsp;tares&nbsp;themselves&nbsp;were&nbsp;called&nbsp;"darnel,"&nbsp;some&nbsp;form&nbsp;of&nbsp;plant&nbsp;or&nbsp;wild&nbsp;corn&nbsp;that&nbsp;was&nbsp;slightly&nbsp;poisonous&nbsp;and&nbsp;narcotic.&nbsp;When&nbsp;eaten&nbsp;it&nbsp;would&nbsp;cause&nbsp;dizziness&nbsp;and&nbsp;nausea.&nbsp;It&nbsp;was&nbsp;called&nbsp;the&nbsp;(illegitimate)&nbsp;wheat.&nbsp;Its&nbsp;roots&nbsp;became&nbsp;intertwined&nbsp;with&nbsp;the&nbsp;roots&nbsp;of&nbsp;the&nbsp;wheat.&nbsp;If&nbsp;it&nbsp;was&nbsp;rooted&nbsp;up&nbsp;it&nbsp;would&nbsp;destroy&nbsp;the&nbsp;wheat&nbsp;plant&nbsp;before&nbsp;the&nbsp;fruit&nbsp;became&nbsp;mature.&nbsp;The&nbsp;method&nbsp;used&nbsp;to&nbsp;get&nbsp;rid&nbsp;of&nbsp;it&nbsp;was&nbsp;to&nbsp;let&nbsp;it&nbsp;grow&nbsp;and&nbsp;then&nbsp;to&nbsp;harvest&nbsp;it&nbsp;with&nbsp;the&nbsp;wheat.&nbsp;It&nbsp;was&nbsp;then&nbsp;separated&nbsp;from&nbsp;the&nbsp;wheat,&nbsp;bundled&nbsp;together,&nbsp;and&nbsp;cast&nbsp;into&nbsp;a&nbsp;flaming&nbsp;fire.</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p17 style="margin-left:36.0000pt; text-indent:-18.0000pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; mso-list:l17 level1 lfo32; " ><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><span style='mso-list:Ignore; ' >7.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >The&nbsp;tares&nbsp;(unregenerate)&nbsp;looked&nbsp;like&nbsp;wheat&nbsp;when&nbsp;sown&nbsp;and&nbsp;during&nbsp;the&nbsp;growing&nbsp;stage.&nbsp;All&nbsp;men&nbsp;appear&nbsp;the&nbsp;same&nbsp;in&nbsp;religious&nbsp;practices.&nbsp;It&nbsp;is&nbsp;during&nbsp;the&nbsp;fruit-bearing&nbsp;stage&nbsp;that&nbsp;the&nbsp;difference&nbsp;appears.&nbsp;Unregenerate&nbsp;men&nbsp;can&nbsp;imitate&nbsp;true&nbsp;believers&nbsp;for&nbsp;only&nbsp;so&nbsp;long;&nbsp;eventually&nbsp;their&nbsp;true&nbsp;nature&nbsp;begins&nbsp;to&nbsp;show.</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p17 style="margin-left:36.0000pt; text-indent:-18.0000pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; mso-list:l17 level1 lfo32; " ><![if !supportLists]><span style="font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><span style='mso-list:Ignore; ' >8.<span>&nbsp;</span></span></span><![endif]><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >A&nbsp;person's&nbsp;nature&nbsp;always&nbsp;comes&nbsp;out&nbsp;eventually.&nbsp;A&nbsp;tare&nbsp;shows&nbsp;itself.&nbsp;A&nbsp;wicked&nbsp;person&nbsp;may&nbsp;profess&nbsp;to&nbsp;be&nbsp;righteous,&nbsp;but&nbsp;a&nbsp;life&nbsp;of&nbsp;selfishness&nbsp;and&nbsp;unrighteousness&nbsp;will&nbsp;eventually&nbsp;take&nbsp;hold.&nbsp;The&nbsp;profession&nbsp;may&nbsp;continue,&nbsp;but&nbsp;so&nbsp;will&nbsp;the&nbsp;life&nbsp;of&nbsp;wickedness.</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p17 style="margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; " ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;9.&nbsp;&nbsp;The&nbsp;tares&nbsp;(wicked)&nbsp;among&nbsp;the&nbsp;wheat&nbsp;(righteous)&nbsp;are&nbsp;hurtful&nbsp;to&nbsp;the&nbsp;wheat.</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p17 style="margin-left:50.4000pt; text-indent:-18.0000pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; " ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >a.&#160;&#160;&nbsp;They&nbsp;are&nbsp;an&nbsp;evil&nbsp;reflection&nbsp;upon&nbsp;the&nbsp;wheat.&nbsp;They&nbsp;sometimes&nbsp;make&nbsp;it&nbsp;very&nbsp;difficult&nbsp;for&nbsp;the&nbsp;world&nbsp;to&nbsp;distinguish&nbsp;between&nbsp;</span><span class="15" style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-style:normal; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >good</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-style:italic; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >and&nbsp;evil;&nbsp;they&nbsp;are&nbsp;the&nbsp;primary&nbsp;cause&nbsp;for&nbsp;the&nbsp;finger&nbsp;pointing&nbsp;of&nbsp;hypocrisy&nbsp;leveled&nbsp;against&nbsp;the&nbsp;church.</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p17 style="margin-left:50.4000pt; text-indent:-18.0000pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; " ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >b.&#160;&#160;&nbsp;They&nbsp;stymie&nbsp;the&nbsp;growth&nbsp;of&nbsp;the&nbsp;wheat.&nbsp;Their&nbsp;behavior&nbsp;and&nbsp;conversation&nbsp;and&nbsp;thoughts&nbsp;are&nbsp;centered&nbsp;in&nbsp;the&nbsp;world,&nbsp;not&nbsp;on&nbsp;Christ.&nbsp;Therefore&nbsp;the&nbsp;righteous&nbsp;are&nbsp;not&nbsp;edified&nbsp;when&nbsp;tares&nbsp;are&nbsp;clinging&nbsp;to&nbsp;them.</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:12.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p17 style="margin-left:50.4000pt; text-indent:-18.0000pt; margin-bottom:0pt; >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:20.0000pt; font-family:'Georgia'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p18 style="margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; " ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >This&nbsp;parable&nbsp;revolves&nbsp;around&nbsp;a&nbsp;man&nbsp;who,before&nbsp;going&nbsp;on&nbsp;a&nbsp;long&nbsp;journey,&nbsp;assembles&nbsp;his&nbsp;own&nbsp;servants&nbsp;and&nbsp;gave&nbsp;to&nbsp;each&nbsp;varying&nbsp;amounts&nbsp;of&nbsp;money.&nbsp;One&nbsp;gets&nbsp;5&nbsp;talents,&nbsp;another&nbsp;2,&nbsp;and&nbsp;the&nbsp;last&nbsp;gets&nbsp;one&nbsp;talent.&nbsp;They&nbsp;were&nbsp;to&nbsp;use&nbsp;this&nbsp;money&nbsp;to&nbsp;bring&nbsp;income&nbsp;to&nbsp;the&nbsp;master.&nbsp;The&nbsp;man&nbsp;with&nbsp;the&nbsp;5&nbsp;talents&nbsp;earned&nbsp;another&nbsp;5.&nbsp;The&nbsp;man&nbsp;with&nbsp;2,&nbsp;doubled&nbsp;also.&nbsp;But&nbsp;the&nbsp;man&nbsp;with&nbsp;the&nbsp;one&nbsp;talent&nbsp;went&nbsp;and&nbsp;dug&nbsp;a&nbsp;hole&nbsp;and&nbsp;buried&nbsp;it.</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p0 style="margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; " ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >Christ&nbsp;is&nbsp;the&nbsp;master.&nbsp;The&nbsp;three&nbsp;servants&nbsp;are&nbsp;Israelites&nbsp;living&nbsp;during&nbsp;the&nbsp;tribulation,&nbsp;responsible&nbsp;to&nbsp;represent&nbsp;the&nbsp;interests&nbsp;of&nbsp;the&nbsp;absent&nbsp;Lord.&nbsp;They&nbsp;are&nbsp;given&nbsp;responsibility&nbsp;according&nbsp;to&nbsp;their&nbsp;individual&nbsp;abilities.</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p0 style="margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; " ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >After&nbsp;along&nbsp;time,&nbsp;the&nbsp;Lord&nbsp;returns,&nbsp;and&nbsp;settles&nbsp;account&nbsp;with&nbsp;them.&nbsp;The&nbsp;1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; vertical-align:super; " >st</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >&nbsp;two&nbsp;received&nbsp;exactly&nbsp;the&nbsp;same&nbsp;acommadation,&nbsp;&#8220;well&nbsp;done,&nbsp;good&nbsp;and&nbsp;faithful&nbsp;servant:&nbsp;you&nbsp;were&nbsp;faithful&nbsp;over&nbsp;a&nbsp;few&nbsp;things,&nbsp;enter&nbsp;into&nbsp;the&nbsp;joy&nbsp;of&nbsp;the&nbsp;Lord&#8221;&nbsp;The&nbsp;test&nbsp;of&nbsp;their&nbsp;service&nbsp;was&nbsp;not&nbsp;how&nbsp;much&nbsp;they&nbsp;earned,&nbsp;but&nbsp;how&nbsp;hard&nbsp;they&nbsp;tried.&nbsp;Each&nbsp;used&nbsp;his&nbsp;ability&nbsp;fully&nbsp;and&nbsp;earned&nbsp;100%!&nbsp;These&nbsp;represent&nbsp;believers.&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p0 style="margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; " ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >The&nbsp;3</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; vertical-align:super; " >rd</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >&nbsp;servant&nbsp;had&nbsp;nothing&nbsp;but&nbsp;insults&nbsp;and&nbsp;excuses&nbsp;for&nbsp;his&nbsp;master.&nbsp;He&nbsp;accused&nbsp;him&nbsp;of&nbsp;being&nbsp;hard&nbsp;and&nbsp;unreasonable.&nbsp;He&nbsp;excused&nbsp;himself&nbsp;on&nbsp;the&nbsp;basis&nbsp;that&nbsp;he&nbsp;was&nbsp;afraid,&nbsp;so&nbsp;he&nbsp;buried&nbsp;his&nbsp;talent.&nbsp;The&nbsp;servant&nbsp;is&nbsp;an&nbsp;unbeliever,&nbsp;no&nbsp;reak&nbsp;servant&nbsp;would&nbsp;think&nbsp;that&nbsp;of&nbsp;his&nbsp;master.</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p0 style="margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; " ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >If&nbsp;this&nbsp;man&nbsp;had&nbsp;earned&nbsp;one&nbsp;talent&nbsp;with&nbsp;his&nbsp;talent,&nbsp;he&nbsp;would&nbsp;have&nbsp;received&nbsp;the&nbsp;same&nbsp;commendation.&nbsp;Instead,&nbsp;all&nbsp;he&nbsp;had&nbsp;to&nbsp;show&nbsp;for&nbsp;his&nbsp;life&nbsp;was&nbsp;a&nbsp;hole&nbsp;in&nbsp;the&nbsp;ground!&nbsp;His&nbsp;talent&nbsp;was&nbsp;given&nbsp;to&nbsp;the&nbsp;man&nbsp;with&nbsp;the&nbsp;ten&nbsp;talents.&nbsp;&#8220;To&nbsp;everyone&nbsp;who&nbsp;has,&nbsp;more&nbsp;will&nbsp;be&nbsp;given,&nbsp;and&nbsp;he&nbsp;will&nbsp;have&nbsp;abundance;&nbsp;but&nbsp;from&nbsp;him&nbsp;who&nbsp;does&nbsp;not&nbsp;have,&nbsp;even&nbsp;what&nbsp;he&nbsp;has&nbsp;will&nbsp;be&nbsp;taken&nbsp;away.&#8221;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p0 style="margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; " ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >Those&nbsp;who&nbsp;desire&nbsp;to&nbsp;be&nbsp;used&nbsp;for&nbsp;God&#8217;s&nbsp;glory&nbsp;are&nbsp;given&nbsp;the&nbsp;means.&nbsp;The&nbsp;more&nbsp;they&nbsp;do,&nbsp;the&nbsp;more&nbsp;they&nbsp;are&nbsp;enabled&nbsp;to&nbsp;do&nbsp;for&nbsp;Him.&nbsp;We&nbsp;lose&nbsp;what&nbsp;we&nbsp;do&nbsp;not&nbsp;use.</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p0 style="margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; " ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >The&nbsp;mention&nbsp;of&nbsp;the&nbsp;bankers&nbsp;in&nbsp;vs27,&nbsp;suggests&nbsp;that&nbsp;if&nbsp;we&nbsp;cannot&nbsp;use&nbsp;our&nbsp;possessions&nbsp;for&nbsp;the&nbsp;Lord,&nbsp;we&nbsp;should&nbsp;turn&nbsp;them&nbsp;over&nbsp;to&nbsp;others&nbsp;who&nbsp;can.&nbsp;The&nbsp;bankers&nbsp;in&nbsp;this&nbsp;case&nbsp;may&nbsp;be&nbsp;missionaries,&nbsp;Bible&nbsp;Societies&nbsp;etc.&nbsp;There&nbsp;is&nbsp;no&nbsp;excuse&nbsp;for&nbsp;leaving&nbsp;money&nbsp;idle.</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p0 style="margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; " ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " >The&nbsp;unprofitable&nbsp;servant&nbsp;was&nbsp;cast&nbsp;out.&nbsp;He&nbsp;shared&nbsp;his&nbsp;fate&nbsp;with&nbsp;the&nbsp;wicked.&nbsp;It&nbsp;was&nbsp;not&nbsp;his&nbsp;failure&nbsp;to&nbsp;invest&nbsp;the&nbsp;talent,&nbsp;that&nbsp;condemned&nbsp;him,&nbsp;rather&nbsp;his&nbsp;lack&nbsp;of&nbsp;good&nbsp;works&nbsp;showed&nbsp;that&nbsp;he&nbsp;lacked&nbsp;saving&nbsp;faith.</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class=p0 style="margin-bottom:0pt; margin-top:0pt; " ><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><br clear=all style='page-break-before:always'></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes'; font-size:18.0000pt; font-family:'Times New Roman'; " ><o:p></o:p></span></p></div><!--EndFragment--></body></html>
